class="noprint infobox" id="GeoGroup" style="width: 23em; font-size: 88%; line-height: 1.5em">\n\n<tbody><tr>\n<td><b>Map all coordinates using:</b> <a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/osm4wiki/cgi-bin/wiki/wiki-osm.pl?project=en&amp;article=Mendip_District">OpenStreetMap</a>&#160;\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td><b>Download coordinates as:</b> <a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/kmlexport?article=Mendip_District">KML</a>&#160;<b>&#183;</b>&#160;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://tripgang.com/kml2gpx/http%3A%2F%2Ftools.wmflabs.org%2Fkmlexport%3Farticle%3DMendip_District?gpx=1">GPX</a>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p><b>Mendip</b> is a <a href="/wiki/Non-metropolitan_district" title="Non-metropolitan district">local government district</a> of <a href="/wiki/Somerset" title="Somerset">Somerset</a> in England. The district covers a largely rural area of 285 square miles (738&#160;km<sup>2</sup>)<sup id="cite_ref-SomersetIntelligenceNetwork_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SomersetIntelligenceNetwork-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> with a population of approximately 112,500,<sup id="cite_ref-SomersetIntelligenceNetwork_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SomersetIntelligenceNetwork-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> ranging from the <a href="/wiki/Wiltshire" title="Wiltshire">Wiltshire</a> border in the east to part of the <a href="/wiki/Somerset_Levels" title="Somerset Levels">Somerset Levels</a> in the west. The district takes its name from the <a href="/wiki/Mendip_Hills" title="Mendip Hills">Mendip Hills</a> which lie in its northwest. The administrative centre of the district is <a href="/wiki/Shepton_Mallet" title="Shepton Mallet">Shepton Mallet</a> but the largest town (three times larger than Shepton Mallet) is <a href="/wiki/Frome" title="Frome">Frome</a>.\n</p><p>The district was formed on 1 April 1974 under the <a href="/wiki/Local_Government_Act_1972" title="Local Government Act 1972">Local Government Act 1972</a>, by a merger of the <a href="/wiki/Municipal_borough" title="Municipal borough">municipal boroughs</a> of <a href="/wiki/Glastonbury" title="Glastonbury">Glastonbury</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wells,_Somerset" title="Wells, Somerset">Wells</a>, along with Frome, Shepton Mallet, <a href="/wiki/Street,_Somerset" title="Street, Somerset">Street</a> <a href="/wiki/Urban_district_(Great_Britain_and_Ireland)" title="Urban district (Great Britain and Ireland)">urban districts</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Frome_Rural_District" title="Frome Rural District">Frome Rural District</a>, <a href="/wiki/Shepton_Mallet_Rural_District" title="Shepton Mallet Rural District">Shepton Mallet Rural District</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wells_Rural_District" title="Wells Rural District">Wells Rural District</a>, part of <a href="/wiki/Axbridge_Rural_District" title="Axbridge Rural District">Axbridge Rural District</a> and part of Clutton Rural District.\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-1"><a href="#Toponymy"><span class="tocnumber">6.3</span> <span class="toctext">Railway stations</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-11"><a href="#Education"><span class="tocnumber">7</span> <span class="toctext">Education</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-12"><a href="#See_also"><span class="tocnumber">8</span> <span class="toctext">See also</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-13"><a href="#References"><span class="tocnumber">9</span> <span class="toctext">References</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-14"><a href="#External_links"><span class="tocnumber">10</span> <span class="toctext">External links</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Toponymy">Toponymy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mendip_District&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Toponymy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>Several explanations for the name "Mendip" have been suggested. Its earliest known form is <i>Mendepe</i> in 1185. One suggestion is that it is derived from the <a href="/wiki/Medieval" class="mw-redirect" title="Medieval">medieval</a> term "Myne-deepes".<sup id="cite_ref-EN_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EN-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> However, A D Mills derives its meaning from Celtic <i>monith</i>, meaning mountain or hill, with an uncertain second element, perhaps Old English <i>yppe</i> in the sense of upland, or plateau.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>An alternative explanation is that the name is cognate with <i>Mened</i> (Welsh <i>mynydd</i>), a <a href="/wiki/British_language_(Celtic)" class="mw-redirect" title="British language (Celtic)">Brythonic</a> term for upland moorland. The suffix may be a contraction of the <a href="/wiki/Old_English_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Old English language">Anglo-Saxon</a> <i>hop</i>, meaning a valley. Possible further meanings have been identified. The first is \'the stone pit\' from the <a href="/wiki/Celtic_languages" title="Celtic languages">Celtic</a> <i>meyn</i> and <i>dyppa</i> in reference to the collapsed cave systems of <a href="/wiki/Cheddar,_Somerset" title="Cheddar, Somerset">Cheddar</a>. The second is \'Mighty and Awesome\' from the <a href="/wiki/Old_English_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Old English language">Old English</a> <i>moen</i> and <i>deop</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Governance">Governance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mendip_District&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Governance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The district falls under the jurisdiction of Mendip District Council. As of the 2015 Local elections the Council remained under Conservative control.\n</p>\n<table class="wikitable">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th>Party\n</th>\n<th>Seats\n</th>\n<th>Net Gain/Loss\n</th></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Conservative\n</td>\n<td>32\n</td>\n<td>+2\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Liberal Democrat\n</td>\n<td>10\n</td>\n<td>-6\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Green\n</td>\n<td>3\n</td>\n<td>-3\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Independent\n</td>\n<td>2\n</td>\n<td>+2\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Settlements">Settlements</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mendip_District&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Settlements">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The five main settlements in Mendip are:\n</p>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Frome" title="Frome">Frome</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Glastonbury" title="Glastonbury">Glastonbury</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Shepton_Mallet" title="Shepton Mallet">Shepton Mallet</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Street,_Somerset" title="Street, Somerset">Street</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Wells,_Somerset" title="Wells, Somerset">Wells</a></li></ul>\n<p>Frome, Glastonbury and Shepton Mallet are the only towns in the district, as Wells has city status and Street has maintained its status as a village  despite a population in excess of 11,000.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Other villages and hamlets include:\n</p>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Ashwick" title="Ashwick">Ashwick</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Baltonsborough" title="Baltonsborough">Baltonsborough</a> -
